     The bed in the Marriott Hotel is quite big. The single bed in the general standard room is 1.2 meters. The single bed in the Marriott Hotel is 1.35 meters. This is not bad.
     The bathroom of the hotel is separated from wet and dry. I don‚Äôt know if it is because of the size of the room. I feel that the space of the toilet is a bit small, but the space for bathing is still ok. The toiletries in the bathroom are still good. I like the smell of its toiletries.
     Although it is a double bed, the bath towels and towels are all three, which is good for us with children
     In particular, I would like to praise the mark at the front desk. The service attitude is very good. After checking in, I specially added my WeChat to let me tell him anything. When I got to the room, I sent him a WeChat, hoping that the room would send a pair of slippers. He gave me a set of toiletries, and helped me activate the car. The next day, I told him to help clean the room, and a waiter came immediately, thank you!
     The location of Qianjiang New Town Marriott Hotel is good. The traffic is quite convenient. The subway can be reached. If you drive by yourself, the hotel has an underground garage.
      In general, Qianjiang New Town Marriott Hotel is not bad, I hope I will stay again if I have the opportunity in the future
